  81. I've purchased just about every hair loss shampoo on the market. To date, Lipogaine Big 3 is my favorite.<br /><br />In order for me to even try a Hair Loss Shampoo, it must contain Ketoconazole. This is just about the only Clinically Proven ingredient to actually help with Hair Loss as its been demonstrated to inhibit the Hormone DHT (Dihydrotestosterone) which is the primary culprit causing Male Pattern Hair Loss. Studies for this are readily available online and I encourage anyone to research this and point to two studies in particular. Firstly, a Study Conducted at the University of Liege, Belgium, 1998 ([...]) &amp; Juntendo University School of Medicine, Japan, 2005 ([...]).<br /><br />Ketoconazole is an anti-Fungal agent contained in the popular anti-dandruff Shampoo Nizoral, which, for many years was the only Ketoconazole Shampoo and used widely off label for hair loss prevention.<br /><br />So what makes Lipogaine Big 3 so good? Well, like Nizoral it contains Ketoconazole, proven to aid in hair loss prevention however, it is much improved upon.<br /><br />Ketoconazole is a harsh ingredient when used on its own as it is a powerful anti-dandruff &amp; anti-androgen. Most shampoo's contain a chemical product known as Sodium Lauryl Sulphate (SLS) that like Ketoconazole, is not harmfull in limited exposures to the scalp and skin. SLS is the agent in soaps and cleaners that causes them to 'Foam' up. When combined with Ketoconazole for sustained periods on the scalp as is needed to receive the anti-androgenic (anti-DHT) effects, these ingredients can cause itching, redness and general discomfort on the scalp. Especially when used daily.<br /><br />Lipogaine Big 3 is firstly free of Sodium Lauryl Sulphate. Secondly, it contains Emu Oil which is a powerful anti-inflammatory agent that helps to mitigate harsh effects of the skins exposure to Ketoconazole. Thirdly, it contains other ingredients that although have not been studied as extensively as Ketoconazole in there anti-androgenic effect, are widely used in just about every hair loss/hair growth shampoo (Saw Palmetto etc.).
